# <a name="required-mobile-diagnostic-data-for-microsoft-teams"></a><span data-ttu-id="f4935-103">Microsoft Teams의 필수 모바일 진단 데이터</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-103">Required mobile diagnostic data for Microsoft Teams</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f4935-104">다음 문서는 Microsoft Teams 모바일 이벤트 목록과 각 이벤트에서 수집하는 속성 목록을 포함합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-104">The following article contains a list of Microsoft Teams mobile events, and lists of properties each event collects.</span></span>

## <a name="events"></a><span data-ttu-id="f4935-105">이벤트</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-105">Events</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="f4935-106">아래에 나열된 모든 이벤트에 대한 공통 속성이 있습니다. 이를 검토하려면 [모든 이벤트와 함께 전송된 속성](#properties-sent-with-all-events)을 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-106">There are common properties for all events listed below, to review them, see [Properties sent with all events](#properties-sent-with-all-events).</span></span>

### <a name="panelaction"></a><span data-ttu-id="f4935-107">PanelAction</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-107">PanelAction</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="f4935-108">PanelAction 이벤트의 속성에 대한 자세한 내용은 [panelaction 이벤트를 사용하여 전송된 속성](#properties-sent-with-panelaction-events)을 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-108">For information on the properties of PanelAction events, see [Properties sent with panelaction events](#properties-sent-with-panelaction-events).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-109">**accessibilityUserConfiguration** - 사용자가 접근성 기능을 토글할 때 사용합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-109">**accessibilityUserConfiguration** - When a users toggles an accessibility feature.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-110">**acknowledgeSettingChange** - 업데이트된 알림 설정 대화 상자에서 업데이트를 승인합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-110">**acknowledgeSettingChange** - Acknowledge an update in the we updated a notification setting dialog.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f4935-111">이는 업데이트 알림을 승인하고 전체적인 알림 안정성을 결정하는 데 사용되는 기능 성공 메트릭입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-111">This is a feature success metrics used to acknowledge update notifications and to determine overall notification reliability.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-112">**actionComposeMenu**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-112">**actionComposeMenu**</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="f4935-113">메시지 확장 사용 생성.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-113">Create message extension usage.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="f4935-114">작업 메시지 확장 사용.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-114">Action message extension usage.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-115">**active_session_banner_dismissed** - 위치 공유 활성 알림 배너가 해제되었습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-115">**active_session_banner_dismissed** - The location sharing active reminder banner was dismissed.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-116">**activityChatClicked** - **활동** 탭에서 비 실시간 채팅을 선택하거나 분할 보기가 표시될 때 트리거됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-116">**activityChatClicked** - Triggered when non-live chat is selected in the **Activity** tab or a split view is shown.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-117">**activityContextMenu** - 활동 피드의 오버플로 작업입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-117">**activityContextMenu** - Overflow actions in the activity feed.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-118">**activityFeedClick** - 활동 피드 항목을 탭하고 봇 채팅으로 이동합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-118">**activityFeedClick** - An activity feed item is tapped on and a bot chat is navigated to.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-119">**activityFeedLongPress** - 피드 항목에서 길게 누르기 제스처를 캡처합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-119">**activityFeedLongPress** - Captures long press gestures on feed items.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-120">**activityFeedSwipe** - 피드 항목에서 살짝 밀기 제스처를 캡쳐합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-120">**activityFeedSwipe** - Captures swipe gestures on feed items.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-121">**activityFilterClick** - 활동 필터 사용법을 캡처합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-121">**activityFilterClick** - Captures activity filter usage.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-122">**activityFilterOptionsClick** - 활동 필터 사용량을 캡처합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-122">**activityFilterOptionsClick** - Captures activity filter usage.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-123">**activityFilterOptionsClicked** - 활동 필터 사용법을 캡처합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-123">**activityFilterOptionsClicked** - Captures activity filter usage.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-124">**activityLiveChatClicked** - **활동** 탭의 라이브 모임에서 채팅을 선택하면 트리거됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-124">**activityLiveChatClicked** - Triggered when chat is selected from a live meeting on the **Activity** tab.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-125">**activityLiveDetailsClicked** - **활동** 탭의 라이브 모임에서 **세부 사항**을 선택할 때 트리거됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-125">**activityLiveDetailsClicked** - Triggered when **Details** is selected from a live meeting on the **Activity** tab.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-126">**activityTabClicked** - 다음 사항 결정에 도움이 됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-126">**activityTabClicked** - Helps to determine if:</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="f4935-127">**활동** 탭이 표시됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-127">The **Activity** tab is shown.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="f4935-128">Teams에서 **활동** 탭 이벤트를 캡쳐.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-128">Teams captures an **Activity** tab event.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-129">**activityTypeDropdown** - **내 활동**과 **피드** 사이를 전환하기 위해 활동 필터 사용법을 캡쳐합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-129">**activityTypeDropdown** - Captures activity filter usage to switch between **My Activity** and **Feeds**.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-130">**addChannel** - 채널을 추가합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-130">**addChannel** - Adding a channel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f4935-131">이 항목은 성공적인 채널 만들기에 대한 성공 데이터를 제공합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-131">This item provides success data around the successful creation of a channel.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-132">**addMember** - **자세히** 메뉴에서 **사용자 초대** 단추 선택을 트리거합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-132">**addMember** - Triggered the **Invite people** button is selected in the **More** menu.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-133">**addMembers** - 팀 또는 비공개 채널에 구성원을 추가합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-133">**addMembers** - Add members to a team or private channel.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-134">**addToCalendar** - 개인 일정에 없는 일정 이벤트에 **일정에 추가** 단추를 선택합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-134">**addToCalendar** - Select the **Add to calendar** button for calendar events missing in private calendar.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-135">**addToList** - 연락처 목록에 연락처를 추가합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-135">**addToList** - A contact is added to a contact list.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-136">**addToMeeting** - 모임 참가자 목록에 **모임에 추가** 단추를 선택합니다(채팅에 참가한 참가자의 경우).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-136">**addToMeeting** - Select the **Add to meeting** button in the participant list for a meeting (for participants who are a part of the chat).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-137">**addUserAsContact** - 연락처의 프로필 카드에 **연락처 추가** 아이콘을 선택하여 연락처를 추가할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-137">**addUserAsContact** - A contact can be added by selecting the **Add contact** icon from the profile card of the contact.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-138">**admitAll** - 대기실 섹션에서 **모두 입장 허용** 단추가 선택된 횟수입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-138">**admitAll** - The number of times the **Admit all** button is selected from the lobby section.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-139">**admitParticipant** - 모임 명단에서 모임에 입장이 허용된 횟수입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-139">**admitParticipant** - The number of times someone is admitted into a meeting from the meeting roster.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-140">**alertsNavAlert** - 피드 항목을 탭합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-140">**alertsNavAlert** - Tapping on a feed item.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-141">**android: null** - 봇 채팅을 음소거 또는 음소거 해제합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-141">**android: null** - Mute or unmute a bot chat.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f4935-142">이는 채팅에 대한 기존의 원격 분석을 향상시키고 응용 프로그램 정보만을 추가합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-142">This is enhancing existing telemetry around chats only adds application information.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-143">**anonymousMeetingJoin** - 익명 참가 제공 이름 페이지에서 **모임 참가**를 선택하거나 이름 대화 상자에서 **확인**을 탭합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-143">**anonymousMeetingJoin** - **Join meeting** is selected on an anonymous join provide name page or **OK** is tapped in the name dialog.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-144">**anonymousMeetingJoinWelcome** - 익명 참가 방문 페이지에서 **게스트로 참가**를 선택합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-144">**anonymousMeetingJoinWelcome** - **Join as guest** is selected on an anonymous join meeting landing page.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-145">**anonymousMeetingPostMeetingChat** - 통화 종료 화면에 사용자가 조회한 채팅 횟수입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-145">**anonymousMeetingPostMeetingChat** - The number of user views of chat from the call end screen.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-148">**anonymousMeetingSignInWelcome** - 익명 참여 방문 페이지에서 **로그인 및 참가**를 선택합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-148">**anonymousMeetingSignInWelcome** - The **Sign in and join** is selected on an anonymous join meeting landing page.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-151">**appKilled** - 응용 프로그램이 종료됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-151">**appKilled** - The application is terminated.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-152">**approveTimeOffRequest** -  FLW(일선 직원) 관리자가 일선 직원의 휴가 요청을 승인할 때 입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-152">**approveTimeOffRequest** -  When a FirstLine Worker (FLW) Manager approves a FirstLine Worker request to take time off.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-153">**assigneeChange** - 새 담당자가 작업 항목에 추가될 때 트리거됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-153">**assigneeChange** - Triggers when a new assignee is added to a task item.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-154">**assignmentPickerClicked** - **할당 대상** 단추가 선택되어 담당자 선택 페이지가 열립니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-154">**assignmentPickerClicked** - The **Assign To** button is selected, opening an assignee picker page.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-155">**assignmentRemoved** - **x**(담당자를 제거하는 유일한 방법)를 선택하여 작업 항목에서 담당자를 제거할 때 트리거됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-155">**assignmentRemoved** - Triggers when an assignee is removed from a task item by selecting the **x** (which is the only way to remove an assignee).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-156">**attachmentAdded** - 작업의 첨부 파일이 성공적으로 추가되었는지 확인합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-156">**attachmentAdded** - Confirms that an attachment in a task was successfully added.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-157">**attachmentDeleted** - 작업의 첨부 파일이 성공적으로 삭제되었는지 확인합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-157">**attachmentDeleted** - Confirms that an attachment in a task was successfully deleted.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-158">**attachmentUpdated** - 작업의 첨부 파일이 성공적으로 업데이트되었는지 확인합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-158">**attachmentUpdated** - Confirms that an attachment in a task was successfully updated.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-159">**audioOnlyLowBatteryBanner** - 배터리 부족 배너로 인해 **오디오 전용**이 선택됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-159">**audioOnlyLowBatteryBanner** - The **Audio only** option is selected due to a low battery banner.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-160">**audioOnlyPoorNetworkBanner** - 연결 배너가 불량하여 **비디오 끄기** 옵션이 선택됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-160">**audioOnlyPoorNetworkBanner** - The **Video off** option is selected due to a poor connection banner.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-161">**audioUserDoubleTap** - 오디오 참가자를 두 번 탭합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-161">**audioUserDoubleTap** - Double tap on an audio participant.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-162">**autoReconnectCallmebackCallDrop** - 종료 화면에서 **콜백** 단추를 선택한 횟수입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-162">**autoReconnectCallmebackCallDrop** - The number of times the **Callmeback** button was selected at a call end screen.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-163">**autoReconnectDialIn**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-163">**autoReconnectDialIn**</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="f4935-164">UFD를 다시 연결하는 데 **전화 접속** 단추가 선택됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-164">The **Dial in** button is selected on the reconnect UFD.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="f4935-165">다시 연결되는 동안 **전화 접속** 단추를 선택한 횟수입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-165">The number of times the **Dial In** button was selected while a reconnect is happening.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-166">**autoReconnectDialInonCallDrop** - 통화 연결이 끊긴 UFD에서 **전화 통화** 단추가 선택됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-166">**autoReconnectDialInonCallDrop** - The **Dial in** button is selected on the call disconnected UFD.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-167">**autoReconnectDialOut** - UDF를 다시 연결하는 데 **콜백** 단추가 선택됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-167">**autoReconnectDialOut** - The **Call me back** button is selected on the reconnect UFD.</span></span>

### <a name="scenario"></a><span data-ttu-id="f4935-1300">시나리오</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-1300">Scenario</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="f4935-1301">PanelAction 이벤트의 속성에 대한 자세한 내용은 [panelaction 시나리오 이벤트를 사용하여 전송된 속성](#properties-sent-with-scenario-events)을 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-1301">For information on the properties of PanelAction events, see [Properties sent with scenario events](#properties-sent-with-scenario-events).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-1302">**create_default_plan_and_nav_to_view** - 기본 공유 작업 목록이 성공적으로 만들어졌는지 확인하고 사용자가 작업 후 결과 보기에 도달하는 데 걸린 시간을 확인합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-1302">**create_default_plan_and_nav_to_view** - Confirms successful creation of a default shared task list and how long it took for a user to land on the resulting view after action.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-1317">**rename_personal_plan** - 개인 작업 목록의 성공적인 이름 변경을 확인합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-1317">**rename_personal_plan** - Confirms the successful renaming of a personal task list.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-1318">**rename_planner_plan** - 공유 작업 목록의 성공적인 이름 변경을 확인합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-1318">**rename_planner_plan** - Confirms the successful renaming of a shared task list.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-1319">**update_planner_task_and_nav_to_view** - 공유 작업 항목의 성공적인 업데이트와 사용자가 작업 후 결과 보기에 도달하는 데 걸린 시간을 확인합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-1319">**update_planner_task_and_nav_to_view** - Confirms the successful updating of a shared task item and how long it took for a user to land on resulting view after action.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f4935-1320">**update_personal_task_and_nav_to_view** - 개인 작업 항목의 성공적인 업데이트와 사용자가 결과 보기에 도달하는 데 걸린 시간을 확인합니다. - **updatePlannerTask** - 사용자가 공유 작업 목록에서 작업을 성공적으로 업데이트했는지 확인합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4935-1320">**update_personal_task_and_nav_to_view** - Confirms the successful updating of a personal task item and how long it took for a user to land on resulting view after - **updatePlannerTask** - Confirms that a user has successfully updated a task in a shared taks list.</span></span>
